China Construction Bank Corporation: Inaugural Meeting of Promoters Held Yesterday 129

Capital of Ten Million Yuan Fully Raised

Founding Meeting Scheduled Within Two Months

The China Construction Bank Corporation, which is actively being prepared, held its first promoters' meeting yesterday morning. The capital of ten million yuan has been fully raised by various banks and individuals. Recently, it is planned to convene a shareholders' founding meeting and proceed with registration with the Ministry of Finance and relevant authorities. It is expected to be formally established within two months. The details are as follows:

Company Business 130

Major Chinese banks and economic figures have established the China Construction Bank Corporation. The motivation for its organization, the raising of capital, and the limits of its management rights are entirely controlled by Chinese people, which is a major tool for economic transformation. The purpose of the China Construction Bank Corporation is to connect domestic banks and overseas financial circles to provide assistance and coordination for public or private enterprises in order to seek the development of industry and commerce, and to focus on the continuous supply of large capitalists. The company specializes in researching any enterprise with new plans, and for those deemed qualified, it will find ways to raise capital from China and abroad, and may act as a supervisor on behalf of investors.

The Promoters 131

The company's promoters and the number of shares subscribed are as follows: Xie Zuokai subscribed 190 shares, Yang Can San, Wang Boyuan, Zou Minchu, Xu Keting, Wang Zihou, Liu Huizhi, Zhang Weiru, Song Ziwen, Song Ziliang, Wu Qiding, Xu Xinliu, Zhang Jia'ao, Hu Bijang, Chuan Zongyao, Xu Busun, Zhang Renjie, Qian Yongming, Sun Zunjiang, Li Yuying, Zhou Zuomin, Chen Huide, Ye Fuxiao, Bei Songsun, Li Fusun, Tang Shoumin, Kong Xiangxi, and 26 others, each subscribed 185 shares. The total number of shares subscribed by the 27 promoters above is 5,000 shares, each share is 100 yuan, totaling 500,000 yuan.

Capital Fully Raised 132

The company's total capital is 10 million silver dollars, divided into 100,000 shares, each share is 100 yuan. In addition to the 5,000 shares subscribed by the promoters, the rest are undertaken by the following banks and individuals: (1) Banks include Central, China, Communications, Jin Cheng, Zhongnan, Shanghai, Zhejiang Industrial, China Industrial, Juxingcheng, Kenye, Tongshang, Dalu, Jiangsu and Zhejiang, Siming, Donglai, Guohuo, Guohua; (2) Individuals include Yong Zhi, Song Ziwen, Zhang Gongquan, Li Fusun, Chen Guangfu, Bei Songsun, Zhang Weiru, Xu Busun. Now the capital has been fully raised as scheduled.

Yesterday's Meeting 133

The company held a promoters' meeting at 11:00 AM yesterday at its head office at No. 7 Hankou Road. Those present included Kong Xiangxi, Song Ziwen, Song Wenliang, Bei Songsun, Zhang Weiru, Chen Guangfu, Xu Keting, Ye Fuxiao, Tang Shoumin, Xie Zuokai, Liu Huizhi, Wu Qiding, Xu Xinliu, and Xu Busun, Qian Yongming, etc. Lawyer Yao Yongli was present as an observer. First, the chairman reported on the progress of the shareholders' fundraising. Then, Yao Yongli reported on the handling of the filing and registration with the Ministry of Finance and the Bureau of Social Affairs. The meeting adjourned at 12:30 PM. It is reported that the company will soon convene a shareholders' founding meeting, which is expected to be formally established within two months.

Organizational Nature 134

According to a promoter, the nature and mission of the company are as follows: China's finance has changed considerably in the past 20 years, because China's banking industry has progressed with the times, enabling domestic and overseas Chinese capital to accumulate and concentrate on China's revitalization plan. It is possible to use the above-mentioned economic development to make cooperation between Chinese and foreign capital possible. Moreover, if this capital can obtain considerable guarantees, it can naturally be supplied for national economic construction. In recent years, although various new enterprises have been formed by Chinese banks and foreign businesses, there is still a lack of a mechanism that enables cooperation between various banks and foreign businesses. This is the origin of the establishment of the China Construction Bank Corporation in the midst of China's economic construction, which means that it has arisen in response to the demands of the times. Because the company's nature is not an investment trust company, the amount of capital raised is not important. According to the precedent of financial organizations, the company can exert its function whenever there is a considerable opportunity to assist China's business enterprises. The company has no intention of directly incorporating foreign capital into the company now or in the future. However, the company takes an open attitude. If there is considerable foreign capital for enterprises, it can cooperate with Chinese investors and the company, or the company can invest in various enterprises on its behalf. Because the company represents the most stable force in China, it is firmly believed that foreign businessmen who are willing to invest in China will be willing to cooperate with the company. The company is a purely commercial institution. Following Dr. Sun Yat-Sen's instructions, it recognizes the use of foreign capital as legitimate cooperation for the development of China's resources and the benefit of mankind. In this spirit of cooperation, regardless of whether it is at home or abroad, it does not involve politics, does not hold prejudices, and takes supporting China's economic construction as its own responsibility. This is also the company's grand vision.

Today's Issuance of the Boxer Indemnity 6% British Gold Bonds: Underwritten by Four Banks, Marketed Domestically and Internationally 135

In order to complete the Guangdong-Hankou Railway, the Ministry of Railways, with the Boxer Indemnity as collateral, in conjunction with the Ministry of Finance, is issuing 1.5 million pounds of the Republic of China's 6% British Gold Boxer Indemnity Bonds today, underwritten by four banks including Bank of China and HSBC, and marketed domestically and internationally. The details are as follows:

Commencement of Issuance: The Republic of China's 6% British Gold Boxer Indemnity Bonds, with a total amount of 1.5 million pounds, are scheduled to begin issuance today. Principal will be repaid from January 1, 1935, and thereafter every six months. The British Boxer Indemnity borrowed by the Ministry of Railways is designated as the fund, and will be submitted to the designated four banks, including the Central Bank, Bank of China, Communications Bank, and HSBC, for storage on schedule for payment. The fund will be managed by the fund management committee composed of the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Railways, the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Trustees, the Audit Department, and the underwriting bank. The bonds are divided into three types: 50 pounds, 100 pounds, and 1,000 pounds.

Four Banks Underwrite: A reporter from the New Sound Agency learned from Shanghai banking circles yesterday that after the issuance of the 6% British Gold Boxer Indemnity Bonds, they will be underwritten by four banks: the Central Bank, Bank of China, Communications Bank, and HSBC. It has been decided that the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Communications Bank will be responsible for domestic sales, while HSBC will be responsible for international sales. The total amount of these bonds is 1.5 million pounds. It is expected that the international sales performance will be very good, because the interest rate on foreign government bonds is 3% to 5%, while the interest rate on these bonds is 6%, which is higher than that of foreign bonds. Moreover, the collateral is the British Boxer Indemnity, which is very reliable.

(Answer) If Ambassador Arima comes to China and I happen to be in Shanghai, private socializing may be unavoidable. (Question) What are your opinions on the reports of local solutions? (Answer) I have never advocated this from the beginning. (Question) What is your opinion on the recent reports regarding the resumption of business of Huie Bank? (Answer) I have been stationed in North China for more than a year and have been in a state of constant crisis and shock. I have not had time to attend to economic matters. I only became aware of this issue recently after seeing the news reports and am currently inquiring about it.

"May 30th" Memorial Day the Day Before Yesterday: The Whole City Flies Flags at Half-Mast in Mourning, All Government Agencies Continue to Work as Usual, Public Cemetery Board Holds Public Memorial Ceremony 137

The day before yesterday, all government agencies and schools in the city flew flags at half-mast to mourn the martyrs who died on May 30th. Jiangnan Paper Mill Welcomed Him Yesterday 147

The Panchen Lama visited the Jiangnan Paper Manufacturing Company factory in Caojiadu at around 4:00 PM yesterday, accompanied by Li Dachao, Section Chief of the Municipal Government. Including the Panchen Lama's attendants, there were more than a dozen people. Yellow sand was spread all the way from the entrance to the office to the upstairs living room, and the floor was covered with yellow cloth to show solemnity. Xie Meicun, Chairman of the Board of Directors, Wu Yaoting, Director, Zheng Shuzhi, General Manager, and Zhu Fujiu, Legal Counsel, cordially received him. They first served tea and snacks and took photos, and then accompanied him to visit the entire factory. The Panchen Lama greatly praised the factory's perfect equipment and excellent products. Before leaving, the company presented him with dozens of paper samples and a roll of brocade yellow satin to express their respect. Meiya Silk Factory Hosted the Dharma Vehicle 148

The Meiya Silk Weaving Factory in this port, as a pioneer in improving my country's silk weaving industry, heard that the Panchen Lama was concerned about the industry, so it specially invited him to visit the main factory on Malong Road. A yellow banner was temporarily hung with the words "Welcome the Panchen Lama." In the conference room, there were models of reeling and weaving machines and a variety of products on display. The Lama arrived at the factory at about 4 o'clock and was welcomed into the reception room by Cai Shengbai, the factory's general manager, who served tea and snacks. Mr. Cai also reported on the factory's situation, saying that he was very honored that the Lama was visiting today. The history of my country's silk industry is long, but now it is declining due to the impact of the global economic downturn and the decline of the rural economy. Our factory was established in the ninth year of the Republic of China. We use new machines and domestic silk to improve weaving. All of our products have always been popular with the Chinese people. This time, the Lama is concerned about the industry during his visit to Shanghai, and we hope to have some guidance and promote it. After speaking, he presented a specially made yellow beauty crepe. Then the Lama replied, saying that he was very pleased to hear that the daily necessities used by the Chinese people are now all made in China. Tibet also produces silk and satin, but they are also in decline because the weaving process has not been improved. Your factory's products are excellent and should be promoted. The Lama also personally inscribed a Tibetan blessing, which means "Three Treasures, More Fortune, Auspiciousness and Good Luck." Then Mr. Cai led him to visit various departments and took photos as a memento. The Lama left and visited the Yabu Er Electric Plant, and went to Yan Fuqing's banquet in Ye Garden in Jiangwan in the evening.

Japanese Envoy Arisima Arrived in Shanghai the Day Before Yesterday 152

According to the Central News Agency, Japanese Minister to China, Arisima Akira, returned to his country last month to report on the situation in China to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and to seek instructions on future Sino-Japanese diplomatic policy. He has now completed his duties and arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday at 3:15 PM, accompanied by his wife, Counselor Motono, and Secretary Yokokawa, aboard the Japanese ship Nagasaki Maru. The ship docked at the Wayside Wharf. The Japanese minister disembarked around 4:00 PM and proceeded directly to his private residence on Bi Xun Road to rest. After the ship docked, more than one hundred Japanese officials and civilians in Shanghai, Wang Changchun, a commissioner from the Shanghai Municipal Government, and Chinese and Japanese journalists boarded the ship to meet him. The Japanese minister shook hands with the welcoming personnel in the ship's hall and then met with Chinese and Japanese journalists, stating,

"I (Arisima referring to himself) am unsure whether I will visit Huang Fu immediately after arriving in Shanghai, as I do not know if Mr. Huang is currently in Shanghai. The date of my entry to Beijing has not yet been decided. However, I may need to travel to Beijing in the near future to meet with Chinese diplomatic authorities. I have not yet considered whether to visit Chiang Kai-shek in Nanchang. In short, I have just returned to Shanghai and will decide after resting briefly."

Regarding Sino-Japanese diplomatic issues, he further stated that the rumors that he had brought instructions from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on this trip were not true. He had not received any special instructions from the ministry. As for the so-called "Water Bird Diplomacy," he was unaware of it and did not know the source of the news reports. When reporters inquired about Japan's opinions on Chinese diplomacy, he responded that due to differences in observation, there were bound to be differences in opinion, but the overall policy towards China was consistent.

Regarding the issues of through traffic and through mail, the Japanese minister believed that the negotiation of these issues would be mainly conducted by the Kwantung Army and the North China local government. He had no knowledge of rumors that the through traffic issue had been resolved and that it would be handled by the International Travel Agency. As for the issue of settling Sino-Japanese debt, this was something that Japan hoped for, but the Japanese side had not made any special requests. The Japanese side currently had no special demands regarding the Sino-Japanese tariff issue, but he had heard that the Chinese government would automatically revise the Sino-Japanese tariff rates. The Japanese minister considered the rumors of direct Sino-Japanese negotiations difficult to explain. The Japanese minister further stated that Japan's policy towards China was always based on goodwill. Unfortunately, after the January 28th Incident, the feelings between the two countries deteriorated. During his recent return to his country, he observed that public sentiment in China had become more moderate than before. However, Minister Arisima declined to express any opinion on the informal declaration issued by the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs on April 17th.

Subscriptions for Public Works Bureau Bonds Exceed Original Amount Several Times Over 153

The Public Works Bureau's 1934 bond issue of 7 million yuan was offered to the public on May 31st. These bonds bore an annual interest rate of 5% and were sold at 102.5% of the face value. After subscriptions opened at 10:00 AM, the issue was fully subscribed within minutes. Therefore, subscription applications were closed after fifteen minutes. It is reported that the total subscriptions amounted to approximately 26 million yuan. After deliberation, the Finance Department intends to allocate the bonds to subscribers at 22.5% of the amount they applied for. It is also reported that a considerable number of Chinese individuals subscribed to these bonds.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Sends Letters to Various Public Organizations; to Be Aware of Counterfeit National Products; Prices Referred to as "Several Yuan and Several Tens of Cents" 156

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent letters to the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, cotton cloth industry, woolen textile industry, dyeing and weaving industry trade associations, and the China General Cotton Mill Association, stating: "Esteemed Sirs, our Chamber has repeatedly received reports from patriotic supporters of national products stating that recently, several new types of piece goods have been discovered on the market: (1) the 'Qinu District' trademark, depicting a woman carrying a large flag, whose products are various rayon flosses; (2) the 'Three Ruyi' trademark, depicting three children, one child sitting high above, holding a ruyi in both hands, two children below, facing each other, four hands together holding a ruyi, four feet together dancing on a ruyi, whose products are small twills and colored cotton cloths; (3) the 'Yang Guifei' trademark, whose products are various colored twill cotton cloths; (4) the 'Three Joys' trademark, depicting three people in ancient attire, one leaning against a window holding a book, one leaning against bamboo admiring the scenery, one sitting on a rock, admiring plum blossoms, whose products are various woolen cloths; (5) the 'Ruifeng' trademark, with the roof and courtyard covered in snow, an old man and a young woman in ancient attire admiring the snow by the window, whose products are fine white cloths. The above-mentioned trademarks all feature Chinese characters and stories. Please verify whether they are national products." Our Chamber has found that the above-mentioned five trademarks do not indicate the place of origin, and the prices marked for each piece or yard do not state "several yuan and several jiao" but "several yuan and several tens of silver," clearly attempting to pass themselves off as national products, revealing a lack of awareness. To prevent patriotic supporters of national products from being deceived, we hereby request that you all be notified to pay attention to this matter. This is of utmost importance.

Director Tao Discusses the Implementation of the Strict Prohibition of Narcotics Regulations 160

According to the Central News Agency, a reporter interviewed Tao Baichuan, Director of the Military Law Department of the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, yesterday to inquire about the implementation of the Provisional Regulations on Strict Prohibition of Potent Narcotics. The questions and answers are as follows: (Question) Have most of the provisions of the regulations been implemented? (Answer) The regulations stipulate that they will be implemented ten days after promulgation and delivery. They have now been implemented since the 27th of this month. (Question) What exactly are the so-called potent narcotics? (Answer) They refer to morphine, cocaine, and other compounds or combinations thereof, such as red and white colored pills. (Question) Will all cases involving potent narcotics be handled by the headquarters in the future? Can the courts in the concessions still handle them? (Answer) All cases involving these narcotics will be handled by this headquarters in accordance with the law. The courts in the concessions are also judicial organs of China and are no exception. It is heard that the Municipal Government has notified them in accordance with the order. (Question) Will crimes committed before the implementation of the regulations be punished in accordance with these regulations or still be handled in accordance with the Anti-Opium Law? (Answer) In accordance with the provisions of Article 2 of the Criminal Law, they should be sentenced in accordance with the Anti-Opium Law. According to the interpretation of the Judicial Yuan's Yuanzi No. 271 of the 19th year, they should be sentenced in accordance with the regulations. It has now been submitted to Chairman Chiang for approval, and all criminal acts discovered before the implementation of the regulations will be handled in accordance with the Anti-Opium Law, and the rest will be handled in accordance with the regulations. (Question) The regulations stipulate that manufacturing, selling, and transporting potent narcotics are punishable by death. If there were such crimes in the past, but they have now ceased, can they be treated leniently if discovered in the future? (Answer) It is best to surrender to the competent authority before being discovered, and then a commutation of sentence may be granted in accordance with the law.

Shanghai County Begins Opium Suppression; Investigate and Report Details Within Ten Days; Confess and Quit Opium Use Within June 161

The Shanghai County Government is actively carrying out opium suppression matters in the county. In addition to establishing the Opium Suppression Committee, it has ordered each district to investigate and report on opium smokers within their boundaries by June 30, so that they can be registered and issued licenses. The operational situation of the committee is investigated and recorded as follows: The organization of the committee naturally includes County Magistrate Pan Zhongjia, Public Security Bureau Xu Yuyin as committee members, and Zhang Jingye, a member of the County Party Department, Huang Yunchen, director of the Property Disposal Office, and Yao Huiquan, a local gentry, as appointed committee members. It also has a secretary and four sections including General Affairs, but due to funding issues, the positions are temporarily filled by the committee members and county government staff. Wei Xizhai, secretary of the county government, has been appointed as the secretary, the head of the first section of the county government has been appointed as the head of the General Affairs section, committee member Xu Yuyin has been appointed as the head of the Investigation section, Shen Zao, a member of the Public Security Bureau, has been appointed as the head of the Licensing section, and committee member Huang Yunchen has been appointed as the head of the Audit section. Other section members and secretaries have also been appointed as investigators and are not temporarily established. Furthermore, party and government service personnel and school staff who use opium are required to report and quit opium use within two weeks from June 1. Those who do not use opium are required to obtain a joint guarantee and submit it for verification. Whether there are any organizations manufacturing narcotic drugs within the territory has been ordered by the county government to the Public Security Bureau and various districts to investigate and report the details within ten days. At the same time, measures for those who use opium to confess themselves are being drafted and announced to confess and quit opium use from June 1 to June 30, and they will be exempted from punishment. In addition, the committee believes that the offenders who use drugs can be entrusted by the Zhenjiang Garrison Headquarters to the local county government for trial. Since this county does not also handle judicial affairs and has no prison facilities, it has reported the special circumstances of this county to the province for approval. In addition, in order to gather ideas and benefit from various opinions, the committee has decided to hold a joint opium suppression meeting on the Opium Suppression Memorial Day on June 3 to discuss everything. In addition, the number of local opium paste shops in the county is currently being investigated by the Public Security Bureau to determine the actual situation before further arrangements are made.

Cross-Border Road Construction; North District Telephone Fee Issue; Public Works Bureau to Find a Permanent Solution 162

Regarding the issue of telephone fees in the extraterritorial road area of the Public Concession, the Japanese Residents' Association recently raised an objection to the Public Works Bureau. According to the report of the Secretary General of the Public Works Bureau to the board of directors, this telephone fee is based on the agreement between the telephone company and the Shanghai Telephone Bureau in April of last year. At that time, the Public Works Bureau had carefully considered this matter. According to the agreement, users in the North District whose residences are adjacent to the extraterritorial roads pay an additional twelve yuan per year to the telephone bureau. Those who are not adjacent to the roads pay an additional sixty yuan. As for the West District, those who are more than one hundred yards away from the boundary line pay an additional thirty yuan per year. These conditions are actually the most favorable conditions that the company could obtain. The difference between the North District and the West District is that the telephone bureau already has telephone poles in the North District, which can supply users by itself. The additional telephone fee, within one year after the agreement, is paid by the telephone company on behalf of the users who pay special municipal donations. After one year has passed, the users should pay it themselves. The agreement can now be cancelled with three months' notice, but now it is being sought to revise and establish a permanent agreement.

According to a survey on May 16, there are approximately 836 Japanese residential houses in the area in the North District. 322 houses have paid the special municipal donation for this spring, and 514 houses have not yet paid.

After discussion at the board of directors meeting this Wednesday, the consensus is that the current conditions cannot be made more favorable. This intention should be used to respond to the Residents' Association, along with the letter from the company. However, it should also be expressed to the association that the Public Works Bureau and the company recognized yesterday that it is necessary to revise and establish a permanent and proper agreement. The Public Works Bureau will do its best to assist the company in its efforts in this regard.

Shanghai-Hankou Locally-Made Soybean Cakes Shipped to Guangdong Were Detained and Have Now Been Released 163

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce previously received a telegram from the Guangdong Miscellaneous Grain Association stating that Shanghai, Hankou, and Wuxi locally-made soybean cakes shipped to Guangdong Province were forcibly identified as imported from Shandong Province by the local tax contractors, resulting in the detention of as many as 18,200 pieces. They were required to pay taxes before being released. The Miscellaneous Grain Industry Association of this port requested the City Chamber of Commerce to telegram the Guangdong Provincial Government to strictly order the contractors to identify the origin of the soybean cakes, release them as soon as possible, and clearly delineate the boundaries of where taxes should be levied and where they should be exempted, so that they would not be detained indiscriminately in the future, so that the industry would not be destroyed. After deliberation by the Southwest Political Affairs Conference of the Guangdong Provincial Government, it was decided that Shanghai and Hankou domestically-produced soybean cakes shipped to Guangdong Province should be exempted from taxes, and those detained should be released immediately. The Guangdong Provincial Chamber of Commerce has been notified to inform the Miscellaneous Grain Association to check and comply, and at the same time, the contractors have been ordered to release the detained soybean cakes. The City Chamber of Commerce has also received a reply telegram from the Provincial Chamber of Commerce, informing the Miscellaneous Grain Association to ship locally-made soybean cakes to Guangdong as usual, so as to avoid unsalable goods.

Ministry of Industry Exhibition; Goods of Shanghai Manufacturers Detained Have Been Returned; Ministry of Railways Agrees to Return the Goods to the Manufacturers After They Are Retrieved by the Ministry of Industry 164

The Shanghai National Goods Factory Union led member factories to participate in the spring national goods exhibition held by the National Goods Display Hall of the Ministry of Industry in Beijing. Due to road transportation issues, the exhibits were detained by the Ministry of Railways. The executive committee members Zhang Zilian, Ma Jisheng, Jiang Zhonghe, and Gu Jiuru went to Beijing to petition. After arriving in Beijing, Zhang and others went to the Central Party Headquarters and the Executive Yuan to petition, requesting that the Ministry of Railways be ordered to return the detained goods as soon as possible, and that the regulations for the exhibition held by the Ministry of Railways in Beiping should be followed, regardless of the grade, and that the transportation costs should be exempted. Subsequently, with the mediation of Section Chief Liu of the Central Party Headquarters and Councilor Chen of the Executive Yuan, and with the efforts of Director Peng of the National Goods Display Hall of the Ministry of Industry, and with the Deputy Minister Liu and Director Liang of the Ministry of Industry, the Chief of the Transportation Section of the Ministry of Railways was invited to the Ministry of Industry to discuss solutions, so as to avoid the expansion of the incident. As a result of the discussion, the detained goods were retrieved by the Ministry of Industry and returned to each factory. The representatives and manufacturers were satisfied. Zhang and others also returned to Shanghai yesterday morning. The detention dispute, which had been delayed for more than a month, was resolved satisfactorily.

Emei Ship Returned to Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon; Grounded for More Than Ten Months; Now to Enter the Dock for Major Repairs 166

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Emei ship, which was grounded on the Huatanzi near Fuzhou in the Chuan River in June of last year, has undergone ten months of rescue, with expenses reaching 110,000 yuan. Finally, the reef at the bottom of the ship was blasted away with gunpowder. On the 23rd of last month, the ship left the reef, went into the river, and then went to Yichang. After some minor repairs, it sailed to Hankou and then to Shanghai. It entered the port at 11:00 AM yesterday. The ship is berthed at the Jin Liyuan Wharf. However, due to the considerable damage to the hull, it still needs to enter the dock for major repairs before it can resume its schedule. The company is now being realistic about the ship repair project, so the ship department has decided to hold a bidding process, with each shipyard offering a price for the repair, and the one with the lowest price will be commissioned. After the ship is repaired, it will still sail on the Chuan River and will not operate on the Beijing-Hankou express train.

Taikoo Company's New Ship Shuntian Arrived in Shanghai from Hong Kong; Reception for Visits This Afternoon; Maiden Voyage to Tianjin Tomorrow Afternoon 167

The British Taikoo Company has built a new ship Shuntian at its own factory in Hong Kong to participate in the North China route. The ship arrived in Shanghai from Hong Kong on the 19th of last month and berthed at the Huatong Wharf in Pudong. Yesterday afternoon, it sailed to Puxi and berthed at the company's former wharf. A reception for all sectors will be held this afternoon at 4:00 PM. The construction and equipment of the ship are recorded below.

Ship Construction 168

The company previously had a Shuntian ship that operated on the North China route, namely between Shanghai and Tianjin. Because the ship was old and the hull was aging, it was no longer suitable in this competitive era. Therefore, a new ship was built at the Taikoo Dock in Hong Kong, named Shuntian. The tonnage and length of the ship are the same as those of the Shenjing ship, but the internal equipment and machine furnace are better than those of the Shenjing. It is 300 feet long, 46 feet wide, and 25 feet high, with a total tonnage of about 3,000 tons. It has two steam engines and boilers, and mechanical coal loading, with a (Blong Tish) rotary machine, a (Baibuke Cox) propulsion wheel, three cargo holds, and two-story cargo holds. The loading and unloading of goods is done with new-style cranes that can lift goods weighing 10 tons. New-style (Lima) driving machinery, a complete set of radio equipment, a cold room, and storage of various food items. The speed is the same as that of the Shenjing.

A Glimpse of Passenger Spaces 169

In addition to carrying goods, the ship also pays great attention to passengers, so the passenger space equipment is very well done. There are 53 first-class rooms, single and double berths, on the promenade deck. The large dining room can accommodate 65 people on the top deck. The rooms are all decorated with oak wood, and the recreation room and smoking room are luxuriously equipped. The promenade deck is spacious to make passengers comfortable. The second-class cabins are at the stern and can accommodate 44 people, and there is a reception room. The steerage can accommodate 60 people. The air in the second-story cabin is full. All passenger space equipment is the best on the North China route.

Invitation to Visit 170

The New Shuntian ship arrived in Shanghai on the 29th and berthed at the Huatong Wharf in Pudong. Yesterday at noon, it sailed to Puxi and berthed at the company's former wharf. This afternoon at 4:00 PM, North China traders, customs brokers, and all sectors will be invited to visit, and refreshments will be prepared. The company has sent invitations in advance. The ship is scheduled to depart from Shanghai tomorrow afternoon on its maiden voyage to Tianjin.

Yesterday Morning, Three Fires in the Southern District 174

At No. 40, Shaonian Road, outside Xiaoximen, the Wu Hua Chang Machinery Factory, opened by Wu Lianqing, a native of Yuyao, has been in operation for many years and has been doing well. However, yesterday at around 5:00 AM, while boiling opium paste in the wooden room on the Jintai platform inside the factory, a spark fell to the floor, immediately causing a conflagration. Fortunately, the nearby patrol police noticed it and immediately reported it to the Western District Fire Brigade, which quickly dispatched fire trucks to the scene to exert all efforts to extinguish the fire. After about half an hour, the fire was put out, with only one room being burned. Afterwards, Zhang Quandong, the police chief of the San Guantang Police Station in the Second District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, went to investigate and took the fire starter Wu Lianqing, as well as a copper pot used for burning opium, back to the district for interrogation. Furthermore, at around 3:00 AM, Ling Quanfu, a local resident residing at No. 8, Wuliquiao, Xinqiao Road, in the Southern District, reported through his pig-raising partner, Tang Youlin from Jiangbei, that the thatched house built by the riverbank had been set on fire, causing it to burn and penetrate the roof. He was awakened from his sleep and fled for his life, reporting to the patrol police at the Liyuan Road branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, who immediately notified the fire brigades of various districts to dispatch fire trucks to the scene to extinguish the fire. It took about an hour to put out the fire. Subsequently, Police Chief Li Zhentu went to investigate the cause of the fire and brought Wu Lianqing back to the district for interrogation. It was also discovered that five thatched houses had been burned down, housing a total of nine households, with over thirty pigs, large and small, being burned to death, resulting in significant losses. In addition, the home of Wu Shifan, a native of Funing, in a thatched house without a number behind No. 507, Zhizaoju Road, in the Southern District, also experienced a fire yesterday at around 4:00 AM, due to a lack of caution. The fire quickly became uncontrollable. The patrolling police discovered it and notified the fire brigades of various districts to dispatch vehicles to the scene. The firefighters immediately extinguished the fire, but sixteen thatched houses were burned down. Subsequently, the police station took the fire starter Wu Shifan back to the district to handle the case together, it is said.

Fire Brigade Service Fee Regulations: Shanghai Municipal Council to Revise 175

The Shanghai Municipal Council's Police Committee, at its previous meeting, considering the rising costs of manpower and equipment for the Fire Brigade, proposed to revise the fee regulations for special services such as rescue and guarding entertainment venues. According to a report drafted by the Chief of the Finance Department, measures have been proposed regarding (1) fire fighting fees for properties outside the settlement that do not pay general taxes, (2) guarding fees and water pumping fees inside and outside the settlement (pumping not during fire fighting), and (3) inspection fees for private fire fighting equipment (a new item, but the amount is very small). After discussion, the committee deemed the proposals appropriate and submitted them to the Board of Directors, which has adopted them for implementation. The revised fee regulations will be announced soon.

Robbery on Tangshan Road Last Night: One Thief Wounded and Captured 179

The Lao Gong Tai cake shop at No. 842 to 844, Tangshan Road, near the Baoding Road intersection, was in the process of closing and settling accounts at around 9:40 PM last night when suddenly three thugs dressed in short clothes arrived. Two of the thugs were armed with pistols, and one was armed with a sharp blade. They knocked on the door, and the shopkeeper, thinking they were customers, immediately opened the door and let them in. Unexpectedly, the three thieves, upon entering, immediately drew their pistols and blades, ordering everyone to be silent. They drove the shop employees into a small room in the back, assigning one thief to guard them, while the others entered the shop and opened the cash register, seizing ten silver dollars and ninety cents in small coins. However, the thieves were not satisfied and went upstairs to break into the bedrooms of the shop employees. As they were preparing to rummage through chests and boxes, one of the employees in the small room downstairs took advantage of the thieves' inattention and escaped through the back door, running to a nearby shop to make a phone call to the Huishan Police Station. The police station immediately dispatched a large number of detectives to the scene, first surrounding the front and back doors, and then knocking on the door and demanding entry. The thieves upstairs, hearing the sound, panicked and fled from the rooms, rushing towards the balcony at the back. One of the thieves jumped from the balcony, and seeing the detectives had arrived, opened fire to resist arrest. The two sides exchanged more than ten shots, and the thief was shot down on the spot by the detectives. The remaining thieves had already escaped. The wounded thief was taken to the hospital for treatment, while detectives were dispatched to search for the remaining thieves.

After Shi Jixiang's Tragic Death: Suspect Surrenders: Police Station Raises Suspicious Points: Dong Qing Tian Resolutely Denies 180

Shi Jixiang, a native of Jiangbei, 45 years old, worked for a living. On May 2nd of this year, at 9:00 PM, while walking past the entrance of the Labor Hospital on Xiaoshadu Road in western Shanghai, he was suddenly attacked by thugs who splashed nitric acid, causing him serious injuries. He was taken to the hospital, but treatment was ineffective, and he died on the 10th. The perpetrator fled. The hospital reported the incident to the police station, which forwarded it to the First Special Court's Procuratorate for examination of the body, ordering it to be placed in a coffin and conducting a strict search for the perpetrator for questioning. This was reported in this newspaper. Now, Hua Detective Shi En of the Putuo Road Police Station, based on a report from the victim's family, said that the case was related to Dong Qingtian, a native of Yangzhou residing at No. 209, Robert Sheng Road. Dong used to be a worker at the Nissin Foreign Cotton Mill No. 12, No. 1416. His father, Mr. Dong, had a dispute with the deceased Shi Jixiang over land sales in the countryside of Yangzhou, accumulating a grudge. When Mr. Dong was dying, he told his son Dong Qingtian that he had died because of Shi and that he must avenge his father in the future. Dong agreed. Therefore, Dong is suspected of being heavily involved in Shi's death this time. Furthermore, it was found that the deceased had only been in Shanghai for three days, having just arrived from his hometown, and had no enemies. However, Dong repeatedly asked for leave from the factory after Shi was attacked. After the 10th, he did not come to work at the factory for a week. On the 24th, Dong suddenly sent someone to the factory, falsely claiming that Dong had died and requesting that wages be paid according to regulations. With all these clues, there was no doubt of suspicion. Therefore, the police station strictly investigated Dong. Dong Qingtian learned about the rumors and, in order to clarify the truth, surrendered himself to the Putuo Road Police Station at 10:30 AM yesterday, accompanied by his lawyer Song Shixiang, declaring that he was not related to Shi Jixiang's death. The police chief, stating that further investigation was needed, detained Dong. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Eighth Criminal Division of the First Special Court. Police Station lawyer Gan Jingxian presented the above situation, requesting permission to detain him for further investigation. According to Detective Shi En's report on the investigation, Dong also had another point of suspicion in this case, namely that after the deceased was injured, a witness, Liu Xitang, passed by western Shanghai on a bicycle one day and suddenly saw three people talking along the way, saying, "This matter is terrible; if that person dies, it will be even more terrible." Liu immediately paid attention. One of the three people, whose face was facing outward, was the defendant Dong Qingtian. Witnesses Liu Xitang and Okada Hidefu of the Nissin Foreign Cotton Mill Nos. 1 and 2 are now available to testify. According to the statements of each witness, when questioned, the defendant Dong Qingtian refused to admit anything. Judge Xiao Xie Fen reviewed the confession and ordered Dong to be detained and rescheduled for further questioning.

Dispute After Divorce Between Painter and Female Teacher: Insistently Invited Home After Encounter: Female Teacher Beaten 181

Chen Huilan, a 24-year-old woman from Panyu, Guangdong, used to work as a teacher in a school and resided at No. 5, Zhifengli, Huanlong Road, in the French Concession. She has now moved to the upstairs of No. 333, Fuxu Road. Last year, she was introduced by a friend to Yang Weichen, a 30-year-old man from the same hometown, whose home is at No. 18, Lane 163, Maisai Er Di Luo Road. He is a painter in an oil painting company upstairs in the Dalu Commercial Building and earns a good monthly income. One is a modern woman, and the other is a Western-dressed young man. When they met, they greatly regretted not having met sooner. Every evening, they often frequented singing halls and dance halls. They went from friendship to marriage on December 2nd, getting married at the Xinghualou Restaurant on Fourth Horse Road. Unexpectedly, not long after the marriage, disagreements arose, and this spring, the two parties agreed to divorce, with a written agreement as proof. Unexpectedly, at 7:30 PM on the 25th of last month, the two parties encountered each other on Hualong Road. Yang Weichen immediately invited Chen Huilan to his residence, saying he had important matters to discuss. Chen, remembering their past affection, followed Yang to his residence on Mai Sai Er Di Luo Road. Unexpectedly, after a disagreement, Yang immediately became violent, beating Chen and tying her hands and feet. He also stripped off Chen's black wool Ge cheongsam and black leather shoes, imprisoning Chen in the room. Later, because Chen shouted loudly, the second wife, Wu Guoshi, went upstairs to dissuade him, and Chen was able to escape. He was sent to the Eighth Criminal Division of the Second Special Court yesterday. First, the police station lawyer Chen Ming explained the case, saying that the defendant had committed the crimes of illegal detention and assault, requesting interrogation. Then, the plaintiff Chen Huilan stated that after the woman divorced Yang, she lived in two separate places. On the evening of May 25th, she encountered Yang on Hualong Road. Later, he falsely claimed to repay the woman's old debts and invited her to his home to collect the money. The woman believed it to be true and followed him. Upon arriving, he did not ask about the situation and beat her, requesting interrogation. When questioned, Yang Qingchen confessed that the names of himself and Chen Huilan as husband and wife were still in effect and had not been divorced. Because he had been out for a month without returning home for no reason, he happened to see her on this day, so he persuaded her to return home to live together. Unexpectedly, the plaintiff was barbaric after returning home, so he was angry and committed the assault. The matter was adjourned, and the defendant was released on bail. A summons was issued for the second landlord to appear as a witness at a later date.

Large-Scale Red Pill Operation Cracked Upstairs at a Le Ye Barber Shop on Zhaozhou Road: Over Ten Thousand Red Pills and Dozens of Pieces of Machinery Seized: Several Thousand Colored Paper Bags with Gourd Trademark: Prime Suspect Mei Shaosheng Escapes and is Being Strictly Pursued 184

Recently, the Detective Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau suddenly received a secret report stating that Mei Shaosheng, a Ningbo native residing in the Hexingli, Xinji Bang Road, Hongkou, and Wang Liangsheng from Tongzhou, as well as Lin Liangrui, Zhang Ruiqing, Li Yongxiang, Zhu Jinnan, and others from No. 8, Wangjia Gou, Pudong, had jointly rented the floor above the Yi Le Ye Barber Shop at No. 13, Heng Anfang, Zhaozhou Road, Nanyang Bridge, and had prepared a large number of raw materials for making drugs, secretly setting up a large-scale red pill drug manufacturing operation. To prevent being discovered, Mei Shaosheng personally supervised the workers, starting production only late at night and stopping work at dawn, producing a shocking number of pills every day, which were sold to various places in the surrounding countryside, making a huge profit. Therefore, Mei Shaosheng had the nickname "Red Pill King" in the outside world. After Detective Team Leader Lu Ying learned of this, he immediately reported to Bureau Chief Wen Hongen, who immediately dispatched a large number of long-term police detectives to the address at around 10:00 PM the night before last to secretly investigate. They first surrounded Yi Le Ye on all sides, and then rushed upstairs, where they found the workers busily making red pills in the pavilion room. Upon seeing the detectives arrive, they all panicked and tried to escape, but were captured one by one by the detectives. Five people were arrested, including Wang Liansheng, Lin Liangrui, Li Yongxiang, Zhang Ruiqing, and Zhu Jinnan. On the spot, a large bag of already manufactured red pills was seized, weighing 21 pounds, about 100,000 pills, as well as a piece of red pill dough weighing 10 pounds. There were also dozens of red pill counting boards, car boards, ovens, splints, large and small sieves, cloth bags, small scales, coffee essence, etc. There were also thousands of colored printed paper bags with a gourd trademark printed on the surface, with the words "New Decoration in August of the 21st Year of the Republic of China, Only This One, No Branches." From this, it can be seen that the drug manufacturing operation had been operating for a long time, causing no small amount of harm. The detectives hired a moving truck to transport the prisoners and drugs to the team, interrogated them, and submitted a document to the Third Section of the General Bureau for further investigation. However, the prime suspect Mei Shaosheng, with his keen sense of information, escaped beforehand. The bureau issued a document to the district offices, strictly ordering them to pursue and arrest him for investigation.

Liu Deqi Sent to Austria to Study Tuberculosis 193

Liu Deqi, a native of Jiangxi, graduated from Xiangya Medical College in Changsha and is currently a professor at the National Shanghai Medical College and Deputy Director of the Tuberculosis Department of the Shanghai Red Cross General Hospital. Mr. Liu has profound medical knowledge and has served at the hospital for many years, saving countless lives. In order to pursue further studies, he has been sent to the Medical University of Vienna, the capital of Austria, to study tuberculosis. He is scheduled to leave Shanghai on the German mail ship Koba on Friday morning (June 1st). It is heard that after completing his studies at the university, Mr. Liu also plans to visit famous hospitals in Britain and the United States to study various types of tuberculosis. In the future, when Mr. Liu returns to China, he will definitely make a great contribution to Chinese tuberculosis.

Municipal Bureau of Education: Order to Suppress "Scientific Spirit Writing" Charts, Request to the Municipal Bureau of Public Safety for Prohibition 194

Since the discovery of "scientific spirit writing" in Shanghai, it has become popular throughout the city. The Municipal Bureau of Education and the Bureau of Public Safety believe that this involves superstition, violates prohibitions, and should be strictly prohibited. The Municipal Bureau of Education has already issued a public notice to strictly suppress it and has requested the Municipal Bureau of Public Safety to strictly enforce it. The original text of the Municipal Bureau of Education's public notice is recorded below: Recently, a type of "scientific spirit writing" chart has been discovered in this city, with a small basin attached and a ghost face drawn in the middle. It is being peddled everywhere, and some are openly setting up stalls to sell it, falsely claiming that it can summon ghosts and immortals to inquire about fortune and misfortune. Ignorant people believe it to be true and flock to it. If such superstitious charts and objects are allowed to spread, it will be detrimental to the ideological and cultural future of the people. In addition to requesting the Bureau of Public Safety to prohibit it, this notice is hereby issued for your information.

The National Goods Showcase Display Competition is an innovation in China. People in the national goods industry unanimously praised it. Theft at Shengtai Money Exchange: Loss of Over 12,000 Yuan 196

Shengtai Money Exchange, located at No. 4 Jin'an Lane, Jixiang Street, east end of Zhengjia Wood Bridge in the French Concession, has been established for many years, with a wide range of business and strong capital. The manager, Zhong Yutang from Shaoxing (32 years old), was suddenly visited by six well-dressed robbers at around noon yesterday. Three of the robbers had handguns and went straight into the shop, threatening with their guns and forcing them to hand over the silver box keys. After obtaining the keys, the robbers pried open the silver box and looted all the cash and silver dollars stored inside. They then fled and disappeared. After the robbers left, everyone calmed down and immediately reported the incident to the Grand Clock Police Station in charge. Chinese and foreign detectives rushed to investigate. It was estimated that the robbers took 2,000 yuan in old Zhili Bank banknotes that are not commonly used in the city, 10,885 yuan in miscellaneous banknotes and silver dollars, 300 yuan in silver dollars, and over 1,200 jiao in silver coins, for a total loss of about 13,200 yuan. After the detectives finished their investigation, they reported back to the police chief and ordered all police stations to pay attention and strictly apprehend the robbers.

Tram Accident: Yang Wang's Broken Leg, Taxpayers' Association Sends Letter to Shanghai Municipal Council Requesting Attention 198

Xinsheng News Agency reports that the Chinese Ratepayers Association of the Shanghai International Settlement sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Council yesterday stating: "Regarding Madam Yang Shuying's letter, stating that her mother, Yang Wang, was returning home from Guangren Hospital in a rickshaw at 1:00 PM on the 21st of this month when she was hit by tram number 59 on line 3 of the Shanghai Electric Tramway Company. Due to the driver's negligence, her legs were severed. She was taken to Guangren Hospital by the police for treatment. Although there have been no major changes, she is still in critical condition. The company's employment of such a negligent driver should be fully responsible. It has been many days since the accident, but the police have not indicated that they will file a public prosecution, and the company has not shown any concern, disregarding the lives of citizens, which is deeply regrettable. We hereby report this to your council, requesting you to uphold justice and provide assistance. We urge you to instruct the Shanghai Municipal Council to order the company to bear the medical expenses and all other responsibilities, and to punish the driver responsible for the accident to uphold humanity and ensure the safety of citizens." The Association believes that traffic accidents should be prosecuted in order to provide fair compensation to the victims. Providing medical expenses is a humanitarian act and a responsibility that those who manage the city should fulfill. We hereby request your council to handle this matter in accordance with the law and instruct the tram company to be responsible for the medical expenses to protect the lives of the people and serve as a warning for the future.

Parcel Receipts Should Be Carefully Signed 199

The Two-Route Administration received instructions from the Ministry of Railways stating: "According to a report from the Longhai Railway Bureau, the signature column on the joint transport parcel receipt held by the train conductor is often not filled in as required. The route, date, and name of the person in charge for each route cannot be verified. Once an accident occurs, inquiries by telegram are time-consuming and difficult to ascertain the truth. It is proposed to issue a notice to ensure careful signing." The second copy of the joint transport parcel receipt, held by the train conductor, has a signature column for each person in charge to facilitate verification. It is imperative to sign it carefully to facilitate verification and clarify responsibilities. In addition to issuing separate orders, it is important to ensure that the signing is carried out meticulously. This order has been forwarded to the Transportation Department for compliance.

Publication of the Journal of Economics by the School of Commerce 200

The Journal of Economics published by the Economics Society of the National Shanghai School of Commerce makes significant contributions to economic theory and contemporary economic conditions. Past issues have been praised by society and widely circulated. It is reported that the journal is currently striving to develop and enrich its content, with contributions from prominent contemporary scholars. The combined fourth and fifth issues have been published. Important articles in this issue include Cheng Shaode's "Economic Conditions in the United States During the Financial Panic of 1933," Wu Chunwu's "A Comparative Study of Böhm-Bawerk's and Marx's Theories of Value," and Xu Yuekun's "An Overview of Rural Credit Cooperatives in Various Countries of the World," all of which are valuable works. The journal is distributed by Shanghai Modern Bookstore, as well as Author's Bookstore, Liming Bookstore, Shanghai Magazine Company, and the Ta Kung Pao Agency. The combined issue is priced at 30 cents, and an annual subscription is one yuan.

Record of the Re-establishment Meeting of the West City Chamber of Commerce 201

The West City Chamber of Commerce has been suspended for over a year, causing various inconveniences to businesses. To promote commercial interests and strengthen relationships, a re-establishment meeting was held at 7:00 PM the day before yesterday on the third floor of Guanshengyuan. Officers were re-elected. Over 160 representatives from various businesses attended. Fang Benzhi, Zeng Moche, and Cheng Daosheng were elected as the presidium. After formal ceremonies, Chairman Cao Mo reported the purpose of the meeting, and former secretary Wei Jie reported on the progress of the re-establishment preparations. The meeting then discussed and decided on important proposals such as the association's location, funding, amendments to the constitution, and rent reduction. Subsequently, all attendees voted to elect executive and supervisory committee members. The results were as follows: Daguangming, Laoda Fang, Guanshengyuan, Shenhe Tai, Huiquan Printing House, Mingyuan, Hongyunlou, Yuelaixiang, Shiye Jiuguo Bao, Hongchangxiang, Dahua Gong, Dashun Gong, Tiannanlou, Meihua Company, Datongsheng, Meimei Company, and Furun Chi, totaling seventeen businesses, were elected as executive committee members. Pengshou Tang, Yifeng, Huayi Company, Brothers Company, and Da Zhongguo, totaling five businesses, were elected as alternate executive committee members. Wuzhou Pharmacy, Tianyuan, New Era, Wu Huiyuan, Chunsen, Zhongyang, and Zhonghua Company, totaling seven businesses, were elected as supervisory committee members. Baotai West City Motor Company was elected as the alternate supervisory committee member. It was also decided to hold the first joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees on June 2nd, as well as the inauguration ceremony. The meeting concluded with slogans and refreshments.

Mother of Ru Baoyi Passes Away 202

The mother of Ru Baoyi, a lawyer at the Shanghai Municipal Council, Madam Yang, was brought to live with Ru in Shanghai. Unfortunately, yesterday (the 30th) at 3:30 PM, Madam Yang suddenly felt dizzy. Ru and his wife personally helped her to bed to rest. They immediately called famous Shanghai doctors to the residence for treatment. However, Madam Yang was old and weak, and medicine could not help. She passed away at 10:00 PM that night, at the age of sixty-six. The Ru family has scheduled the encoffining ceremony for 2:00 PM on June 1st at the Chinese Funeral Home on Haige Road. The coffin will be returned to Wujiang, the ancestral home, in a week. Many relatives and friends of Ru are visiting to offer condolences.

Record of the Meeting of Rickshaw Pullers' Representatives 207

Representatives of rickshaw pullers in Shanghai held a joint meeting at a school on Jianwei Avenue the day before yesterday at 3:00 PM. Over 100 people attended, including He Linsheng, Xu Zhulin, and Shan Tianfu. Chen Guoliang was elected as chairman. The chairman reported the purpose of the meeting, stating that rickshaw pullers have repeatedly suffered from theft, extortion, and police abuse. These issues were causing great suffering and losses to rickshaw pullers throughout Shanghai, so it was necessary to discuss relief measures. Xiao Jinfan, Wang Xingyong, Zhu Lin, Wang Yingming, and He Linsheng spoke in succession, stating the need for rickshaw pullers to form a self-organized relief association to thoroughly resolve all issues. As a result of the discussion, Zhou Chunfu and others were elected as members of the preparatory committee, and Hang Zhuqing was elected as an alternate member to be responsible for the preparatory work. At that time, the chairman presented the resolution of the Shanghai Municipal Council's Rickshaw Management Committee regarding photographing and registering rickshaw pullers in good health, and setting the fare for passengers at a minimum of one dime, 2 cents per mile, and 6 cents per hour. The meeting unanimously opposed registration. The meeting then adjourned.

Compilation of Bank Inspection Reports 208

The 75th Inspection Report of the Note Issuance Reserve Inspection Committee of the Bank of China states: In accordance with the rules, the committee inspected the special reserve vault for note issuance and interbank withdrawals of the Shanghai Bank of China and its branches on May 27, 1934. Xu Kan, Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance, Wang Yansong and Pei Yunqing, representatives of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Hu Bijang and Wang Zhixin, representatives of the Shanghai Banking Association, Wang Huailian and Qian Huansheng, representatives of the Shanghai Money Guild, Zhu Huisheng and Qi Ziquan, representatives of the note-receiving banks and shops, and Chen Guangfu, Xu Jili, and Li Zhilian, representatives of the Bank's Board of Directors and Supervisors, along with accountant Wang Zikang, conducted the 75th inspection at the Bank. The results of the inspection are listed on the left: Total amount of notes issued: 107,183,182 yuan, including: 71,600,231 yuan issued by the Bank, 18,530,956 yuan withdrawn by branches, and 17,049,995 yuan withdrawn by banks and shops. Except for the portion withdrawn by banks and shops, which will be inspected separately in accordance with the original method, the inspection of the interbank portion is as follows: Amount issued by the Bank and withdrawn by branches: 90,133,187 yuan. Amount of reserves for the Bank's and branches' notes: 90,133,187 yuan, including: 56,613,714.37 yuan in cash reserves, and 33,519,472.63 yuan in guarantee reserves. The above two items, totaling 60% in cash reserves and 40% in guarantee reserves, have been inspected and found to be accurate. In accordance with Article 5 of the rules, this report is formally submitted. The Republic of China.

May 27, 1934.

The Four Banks Reserve Vault is jointly established by the Yanyeh, Jin Cheng, Zhongnan, and Dalu Banks to exclusively handle the issuance of Central Bank of China notes. In accordance with the Vault's issuance regulations, notes are issued with full reserves, with cash reserves accounting for at least 60% and guarantee reserves accounting for up to 40%. A public announcement is made every week, and the announcement is audited by the four banks' auditors and accountants. The 230th public announcement of the Shanghai Reserve Vault on May 26, 1934, is recorded below: Amount of notes in circulation: 23,476,687 yuan. Total amount of reserves: 23,476,687 yuan, including: 19,125,187 yuan in cash reserves, and 4,351,500 yuan in guarantee reserves.

Lingnan Lin Jieru Comes to Shanghai to Sell Paintings: The painter Lin Jieru, named Baiyun Shanren, is proficient in Chinese and foreign painting methods, integrating all schools into one, with a unique style. He depicts everything from landscapes, figures, insects, fish, birds, and animals in detail, making them come alive on paper. His vigorous brushwork, harmonious colors, and profound creativity are enough to make him famous. In the year of Dingmao, he once traveled to Shanghai. At that time, the late painters Wu Changshuo and Zeng Nongran all recognized his works as surpassing others in Chinese painting. His reputation in Longmen has long been established. This time, he is a returning guest to Shanghai, continuing to sell paintings and broaden his connections. It is heard that he will first donate fifty painted fans, each charging 40% of the ink fee. Items can be sent to Jiuhua Tang, Yichun Tang, Duoyunxuan, Guangya Tang, North Sichuan Road, and major fan shops in this city.

Lawyer Yang Shaozhi Moves: Lawyer Yang Shaozhi has been practicing law in Shanghai for many years, and his business has always been prosperous. It is now heard that Lawyer Yang has moved to 22 Rue Luba Po Poe on June 1st due to the original location being unsuitable, and will continue to practice law there as usual.

Medical and Pharmaceutical World 212

The Original Dafang Hospital Doctor Continues to See Patients: Dr. Fang Juying has established Dafang Hospital in the French Concession of Shanghai for more than ten years, and has won the approval of society. Later, due to being unable to manage it, he canceled the name of Dafang Hospital two years ago and changed it to a private clinic. Recently, however, there have been those who claim to be able to treat venereal diseases, also calling themselves Dafang Hospital. The outside world is unaware and has been greatly misled. In fact, Dr. Fang Juying has nothing to do with them. Dr. Fang's clinic is now located in Xinmin Village, at the intersection of Rue Massenet and Avenue Lafayette, telephone number 83848. The clinic hours are from 3 to 7 pm. All old friends of the former Dafang Hospital who wish to see a doctor can contact Dr. Fang's clinic in Xinmin Village to avoid being misled.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 pm yesterday stated that the northeastern part of China and Shandong are cloudy and clear, with southeast winds and fog in several places. The middle reaches of the Yangtze River and the surrounding areas have strong southeast winds, and there may be thunderstorms tonight. The area south of Ma'anshan Island is cloudy, with localized fog and uncertain wind direction, which is quite gentle. Also, in the 24 hours before 3 pm yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 86.0 and the lowest was 68.0. On the same day last year, the highest was 84.4 and the lowest was 62.1.

Reading Problems

Reading Problems of People with Excessively Mobile Lives 215

丨Reply to Wang Qiang, Li Guisheng, Ah Si, and Xiao Heizi丨

Recently, we received four unexpected letters. The writers are a newspaper vendor, a sailor on a ship, and two others: one is a chauffeur in a private house, and the other is a ticket seller on a tram. According to their sincere letters, they are all avid readers of this column. They told me that their common living conditions make them feel dissatisfied with the reading Q&A. Because the reading Q&A clearly overlooks people with their living conditions. They do not have a relatively stable life, cannot have a relatively long reading plan, and not only that, they cannot even have the conditions to continue reading a book of five hundred pages. But they are still young and still demand knowledge. They also said that their environment is really too bad, too mobile, and they don't know what to do. Although they inevitably have doubts and anxiety about their current lives, they have not despaired. They ask us to answer them and ask (Reading Q&A) to pay attention to the reading problems of mobile people. After reading their four letters, we can't help but feel extremely ashamed. Needless to say, we sympathize with them very much.

We decided that (Reading Q&A) should pay attention to discussing the issues raised by these people in the future, and this article will serve as the beginning of the discussion!

Can people with excessively mobile lives not learn well? No! Absolutely not! Our interpretation of the word (reading) should not deviate from each person's environment and engage in abstract speculation on this word. Saying (reading) should have certain conditions, and (reading) will have certain benefits. Such static observer's remarks are only suitable for university lecture halls and the sofas of ladies' reception rooms as materials for (chat) (tea talk). For people lacking sufficient conditions, it is not only useless but also makes (heroes feel discouraged). What we are talking about (reading) is not empty talk about (reading), but (reading) under certain living conditions, it is a concrete (reading), not (reading) separated from personal practice. If so, then under any living conditions, the (reading) problem can be specifically raised, and there is the possibility of (reading). For example, the above four gentlemen are all people with the most unstable lives, but can't they read because they are unstable? This is a misunderstanding caused by static views. Selling newspapers, working as a sailor on a ship, being a private chauffeur, and selling tickets on a tram are not completely without free time. As for living too mobile and too chaotic, and not having a peaceful mind, so it is not suitable for reading, that is also a formal view. Some people cannot read without a quiet place, and are unwilling to read without a long time, which are all mistakes. It must be known that the current social life cannot allow you to have a quiet life or a stable life. If you wait for that kind of condition, it is tantamount to waiting for (bread to fall from the sky), and you will only fail. Taking the sailor on a ship as an example, first, you must immediately develop the habit of not being afraid of noise. Even if the noise is loud, I can still be at ease. When the ship arrives at a certain pier, you can safely read for a day or two. Moreover, there are quite a few knowledgeable people among the passengers on the ship. If you really work hard and are not ashamed to ask questions, who would not be happy to teach you? How can you not have reading conditions! Let's talk about private chauffeurs! In addition to sending the owner to the office or dance hall, your car is always resting for several hours. Aren't you very free? When your car is parked in the street, don't listen to the jazz music of the dance hall, you can take out the book you want to read from under the seat cushion and read it quietly. Naturally, the other two types of employees still have the possibility of reading in their lives. As for not being able to make a long-term plan, why not shorten it? A year is too long, can you make it three months? If you can't finish reading a large book of four or five hundred pages, why not use a small book of one or two hundred pages? You should do everything according to the practice and possibilities of your life. Don't use the environment to accommodate the book, but use reading to accommodate the environment. A friend of mine told me that in order to read, he plans to resign from his job, which is completely wrong, and does not understand the logic of life. We should not have a negative attitude towards current difficulties, not only in terms of reading. We should try our best to use the conditions that are obviously not available for reading. If Grandpa has only half an hour a day, I will use half an hour. If there is not even half an hour, I will save two or three ten minutes from my sleeping and eating time. We should create the conditions for reading. We should turn the conditions that are unfavorable to us into conditions that are beneficial to us, and transform the current bad environment into a new and better stage. Our life logic is continuous creation, not staying at a certain stage, looking at it and there is no way, stopping and sighing. Napoleon said that there is no difficult word in his dictionary. He is a person who has read the logic of life. The only thing in the world that can be called happy is the success gained after overcoming difficulties, not the person who enjoys the achievements of his ancestors. He never stops in front of obstacles, he dares to face difficulties and is not afraid of failure. People who succeed in reading are almost not people who have all the comfortable conditions, but people who have reached step by step through many dangers and difficulties.

Therefore, we thought that many readers have given up on the reading reports we have made. They often use the current difficulties as an excuse for not moving forward, which is very regrettable. They often exaggerate the difficulties, formally talk about reading, and separate reading from their own lives. These are all harmful concepts for reading and must be removed quickly!

Our reading guidance department does not offer abstract (reading). That is, the various articles on reading methods published in this column have always been intended as reference for everyone, not to be mechanically applied by readers. For example, I have repeatedly provided readers with reading lists for various subjects. We do not want everyone to do that. Readers should dissolve our guidance according to their own living environment and take in the parts they need. We also have different answers for each person who comes to ask for reading guidance, because each person's living conditions are different, and a formula should not be mechanically prescribed.

We cannot wait for good conditions to fall from the sky, and we should not retreat in the face of difficulties. We hope that the four gentlemen will quickly decide on a reading plan with the lowest and shortest time, and then have further discussions with us.

Finally, we dare to say to everyone that knowledge should be obtained bit by bit anytime and anywhere. As long as you don't reject knowledge, not only in books, but all aspects of society are the raw materials you can absorb.

Shanghai Secondary School Sports Federation Athletic Meet to Be Held Today and Tomorrow 216

Starting at 1:30 pm today at the China Athletic Field

More than 200 athletes from 12 boys' schools and 6 girls' schools

The Shanghai Secondary School Sports Federation's men's and women's track and field competition is scheduled to be held this afternoon (Friday and Saturday) at the China Athletic Field. All the arrangements have been prepared by Zhuang Shihong (Chairman), Jiang Jingnan, Wu Lisheng, and other track and field committee members. A total of twelve schools for boys, with 191 athletes, and six schools for girls, with 52 athletes, are participating in this competition. The announcement is recorded below for the attention of all schools.

Pay Attention to the Order of the Venue 217

All competitions will be held according to the scheduled time. It is hoped that the athletes from each school will be on time. Athletes who have no competition should not stand in the middle of the field to watch. Athletes who have finished the competition should not stay in the field. It is hoped that the instructors of each school will inform the athletes in advance, and that each athlete will strictly abide by this rule, and be responsible for maintaining the order of the venue. If there are any athletes holding running shoes and wearing sportswear watching and staying in the field without competition, once discovered, the organizing committee will cancel their competition qualification. It is hoped that all athletes will pay attention. After the opening ceremony, the competition will begin immediately, and there will be no parade ceremony. Each school will be issued two staff badges for entering and leaving the venue. Except for the staff, no other persons may enter the venue. Violators will be punished in the same way as the athletes of each school.

Three Important Announcements 218

(1) There is no athlete lounge in the venue. Each school must find a way to set up Boy Scout tents on the field for rest. (2) Members of this association who hold the school flag and enter the field in formation will not be sold tickets. All others will be sold tickets for four cents each. (3) All sports equipment will be provided by the association, but pole vaulting poles must be provided by each school.
