Telecommunications Special Issue Fourteenth Issue Published Every First and Sixteenth Day

On Arrears of Official Telegrams 283

— Zhen

In an article published in this journal, Mr. Lü Bing discusses "the pauperization of telegrams." Based on telegram business statistics, official and military telegrams account for more than 70%, commercial telegrams account for 20%, and private telegrams account for less than 10%. He argues that telegrams are aristocratic and are the reason why China's telecommunications industry cannot develop, which is a valid point. However, the congestion of official and military telegrams is actually due to the tense military work, frequent transfers, and numerous military dispatches. Only telegrams can be relied on. When the political situation is clear and the military affairs are over, official telegrams will naturally decrease. The telecommunications authorities feel the pain most acutely not because of the large number of official telegrams, but because many official telegrams are not paid for.

Although China's telecommunications is said to be operated by the state, it has not received any subsidies from the national treasury. Therefore, its business policy has to be self-sufficient. It relies solely on telegraph fee income for funding. The maintenance of lines, the purchase of materials, the salaries of employees, and the administrative expenses all require huge sums of money. When there are more commercial telegrams, it can still be勉强 supported. However, in recent years, the domestic economy has gone bankrupt, all industries are depressed, and the telegram business has declined accordingly. Salary arrears are common in the majority of cases, and it is difficult to maintain the status quo. The way to increase revenue and reduce expenditure is to sort out the arrears of official telegrams.

The following table compares official and commercial telegrams for the years 19, 20, and 21.

Comparison Table of the Number of Words in Domestic Official and Commercial Telegrams

Year, Chinese Government Telegrams, Foreign Language (i.e. Official Telegrams)

Year, Chinese Government Telegrams, Foreign Language (i.e. Official Telegrams)

Nineteenth year, 96,450,624, 788,816

Twentieth year, 106,058,809, 703,043

Twenty-first year, 99,462,349, 599,122

From the above table, it can be seen that the number of official telegrams is more than twice that of commercial telegrams every year. The quantity is so large, and many are prefixed with the words "Urgent" and "Limited to Immediate Arrival," which are as urgent as sparks of fire and should be sent in advance. Although commercial telegrams pay cash, they have to be backlogged behind. Therefore, when military affairs are tense, commercial telegrams are often delayed.

Official telegrams only charge half the fee, which is already cheaper than commercial telegrams. Recently, due to the suppression of bandits, there are provisions for material fees for military telegrams, charging only five cents per hundred words. If the payment can be made in accordance with the regulations, the telegraph bureau can still be funded a little, increasing the repair of lines, improving machines, increasing manpower, and improving equipment, then there will be no backlog of commercial telegrams. However, in fact, even the few cents of material fees that should be paid are often not paid. According to telecommunications statistics, the total revenue and expenditure of wired telegraphs in the 19th year had a surplus of more than 3,354,000 yuan, while the arrears of official telegrams reached more than 3,440,000 yuan. In the 20th year, the book surplus was more than 4,928,000 yuan, while the arrears of official telegrams reached more than 4,850,000 yuan. From the establishment of the National Government to December of the 21st year, the arrears of official telegrams totaled more than 16,977,000 yuan. Last year's arrears were also around 3 million yuan. When we read this statistical figure, we should be shocked and amazed at the difficulty of maintaining telecommunications.

There are several reasons for the arrears of official telegrams: (1) Due to the habit of previous years: In the era of warlord governments, the telecommunications bureau was regarded as a tax revenue agency, and the director was mostly appointed by them, so the army's telegrams were permanently recorded in the account. Even if it was not appointed by them, in order to maintain relations with the warlords and preserve their position, they did not dare to demand payment for the arrears of official telegrams, letting them be natural. Therefore, the military believes that free telegrams are a privileged right, and the telecommunications bureau also believes that military telegrams have a precedent for preferential treatment. Some military forces even force the telecommunications bureau to send telegrams without paying a penny, on the pretext of military emergency. If they argue with them, they are accused of "interfering with military opportunities." This kind of bad habit has been going on for a long time. (2) Due to frequent private corruption: The telecommunications bureau has previously adopted a laissez-faire policy for official telegrams, and unscrupulous supervisors take this opportunity to engage in private corruption, either reporting more and less, or concealing the entire number of reports, or requesting the military to give them private subsidies or private errands as conditions for waiving telegram fees. Or the telecommunications bureau and the military personnel in charge collude to cheat, deliberately making things difficult, and when urging for collection, they manipulate each other, and when calculating, they collude with each other. Huge sums of money go into private pockets, and telegram fees are still in the public account. The telecommunications bureau has the name of arrears, and the military has no savings. Now, after several thorough investigations by the Ministry of Communications and severe punishment, this trend has been slightly curbed. (3) Due to the financial difficulties of the sending agencies: In recent years, military affairs have been frequent, the number of troops is large, the national treasury is empty, and the military pay is in arrears, resulting in financial difficulties for various agencies and troops, and the failure to pay the telegram fees in full is also one of the reasons for the arrears.

The telecommunications economy is struggling entirely because of the arrears of official telegrams. If all the payments are made in cash as described above, the annual revenue of the telecommunications administration will increase by at least two to three million yuan. If this huge sum is used to build new lines, add new machines, train key personnel, and sort out telecommunications assets, everything will be plentiful and all industries will be revived. If so, it will also be possible to continue to reduce the current quotation slightly to facilitate the public. If official telegrams cannot be paid in cash, then the telecommunications expenses are entirely borne by the general public who send telegrams, which is unreasonable. In addition to the accumulated losses, there will inevitably be a day when the national telecommunications will go bankrupt. This not only violates the principles of national public enterprises, but also violates the principles of national economy.

The Ministry of Communications is now paying close attention to official and military telegrams. On the one hand, it is vigorously implementing the method of charging and restricting official and military telegrams in order to crack down on them. On the other hand, it is strictly rectifying the method of assessing and examining the charging of official and military telegrams in order to show punishment and encouragement. On the other hand, it is investigating and deducting private official telegrams and recovering telegram fees. In recent years, it has achieved some success. The forced telegrams mentioned in the previous section are not common, and those who engage in private corruption do not dare to test the law. In the future, the political situation will gradually get on track and military affairs will also be calmed down. Perhaps the receipt of official telegrams in cash can achieve a satisfactory purpose?

China-Japan Wireless Telegraph Communication Will Begin Directly Today! 284

— Qinghua

Since the establishment of the Shanghai International Radio Station of the Ministry of Communications in January of the 18th year, it has made extraordinary efforts to develop international radio telegraph business. Therefore, there are now 11 communication circuits including Shanghai-Hong Kong, China-Philippines, China-Netherlands, China-United States (one for the Transportation Company and one for the Mackay Company), China-Germany, China-France, China-Switzerland, China-Vietnam, China-Russia, and China-UK. Among the countries in the world, almost all those with important business relations with China can be reached directly, which not only benefits the commercial people but also greatly assists China's operating enterprises economically. However, what we still regret is that Japan has not yet opened a direct wireless circuit with China, which is a fly in the ointment. The telegrams between Japan and China account for four to five million words each year, accounting for the first position in China's international telegrams. Now, almost all of these telegrams are transmitted by submarine cable. The Ministry of Communications, seeing this, has decided to open the China-Japan wireless circuit starting today. From now on, the telegrams between China and Japan can also be transmitted by radio. China's international radio telegraph business will have a long-term development!

China's domestic telegram business income has gradually declined in recent years due to the depression of industry and commerce, the disturbances of the Communist bandits, and the influence of provincial long-distance telephone. Each telegraph bureau is almost in a difficult situation to maintain. Fortunately, the international radio telegram business has been very good in the past two years, so it has been able to make up for the deficit. Starting from January this year, in order to reduce the burden on the people and develop the business, the Ministry of Communications has specially reduced the price of Chinese telegrams by charging for the name and address. After the implementation of this measure, it is estimated that the income will have to be reduced by 400,000 to 500,000 yuan per year. At this time of economic exhaustion of the telecommunications administration, it must be quickly sought to compensate for it. As for the method of compensation, since there is no possibility for development in the domestic telegrams, the only way is to actively develop international radio telegrams to make up for the insufficiency of domestic telegram income. The urgency of opening the China-Japan circuit is also one of the important reasons!

The prices of telegrams between China and Japan vary from place to place. In order to make it easier for readers to understand, a table is specially listed as follows:

Location of Communication, Total Price per Word, China's Local Line Fee, Japan's Local Line Fee, Submarine Cable Fee, Remarks

Shanghai and Japan, 75 centimes, 20 centimes, 20 centimes, 35 centimes, Qingzuo submarine cable transfer is limited

Qingdao and Japan, 1 franc 25 centimes, 25 centimes, 50 centimes, Qingzuo submarine cable transfer is limited

Other places and Japan, 1 franc 25 centimes, 50 centimes, 25 centimes, 50 centimes,

The submarine cable fees listed in the above table, except for the Qingzuo submarine cable fees, which are equally divided between China and Japan, are entirely earned by the submarine cable company, which amounts to about 2 million yuan per year. The opening of the China-Japan wireless circuit will undoubtedly be of great benefit to the telecommunications economy.

Research on the Application of Shortwaves in Wireless Communication (2) 285

— Wang Dachun

The longest radio waves, with a frequency of ten to one hundred kilocycles per second, are best suited for long-distance international radio telegraph communication, because they are accurate, reliable, and not much affected by the atmosphere. This long wave, with a frequency of fifty kilocycles per second, can be used to transmit radio telephone, such as the transatlantic radio telephone from London to New York, which is one of the examples.

The frequency is from two hundred to two thousand kilocycles per second. This kind of radio wave is actually suitable for short-distance communication and is more suitable for broadcasting. Radio waves around two hundred kilocycles per second have the same properties as long waves, and the accuracy of transmission is no different from that of long waves. Higher frequencies, such as around two thousand kilocycles per second, often experience multiple changes in the strength of the electromagnetic field on the receiving side during the day. Because of this characteristic, the effect is weaker.

Shortwaves are now increasingly valuable for long-distance communication. This frequency is roughly from three thousand to twenty-five thousand kilocycles per second, and higher frequencies are more suitable for use.

When electrical engineers study the propagation characteristics of radio waves, the distinction between "long waves" and "shortwaves" is roughly explained as follows: The electromagnetic waves of long waves are transmitted directly from the transmitting end to the receiving end. As for shortwaves, all electromagnetic waves generated by the transmitting end are reflected by the high-altitude electron layer (IoniasdLayer) and then broadcast to the receiving end.

From experience, radio telephone using shortwaves also has its drawbacks. The electromagnetic field on the receiving side often changes due to the difference between day and night, the difference between seasons in a year, and the different paths of light and dark in the transmission circuit, which affects the sensitivity. However, this change can be reduced to a minimum. An automatic volume controller (AutomaticVolumeControl) can be installed on the receiving side to adjust the amplifier according to the height of the sound waves of the received signal. In addition, there are better methods, using various different frequencies in the same circuit, and making effective adjustments at any time according to the changes in the environment.

The most valuable point of shortwave radio is that it has a direct effect. Its broadcast radio waves can select a certain direction and transmit on one side. As for long waves, the height of the antenna must be determined according to the applied wavelength. In order to make it direct on one side and achieve good results, even with heavy mechanical equipment and huge capital investment, it may be difficult to achieve satisfactory success. For example, the latest shortwave radio telephone uses a concave mirror with a small hole in the middle. The radio waves are concentrated on the hole due to the concavity of the mirror and transported to the electron layer in the sky, which is reflected to the remote receiver. If this theory is implemented using long waves, the circular surface of the concave mirror must be twice the wavelength, and its diameter must be at least several hundred meters. The width of the antenna network must be several times the wavelength, and its height will reach five thousand meters. This is not allowed by reality, so long waves cannot be used. In modern shortwave radios, the ratio of the length and wavelength of the antenna is ten times, and the height is two times. This ratio is absolutely no problem for radio waves below ten meters. For radio waves exceeding one hundred meters, it is absolutely difficult in practice. Therefore, shortwaves are comparatively valuable.

Modern radio transceivers using reflector and directive antennas have become a common fact. This method can increase the broadcast rate by 15 (Decibels) compared to the non-directional method, so it really increases the efficiency in radio communication.

How Can Telegrams Be Expedited? 286

— Qing

The effectiveness of a telegram lies in its speed, so telegrams can also be called "speedy reports." If a telegram is slow, it not only loses its effectiveness but can also lead to important matters being delayed. Therefore, the sole responsibility of the telegraph office is to deliver telegrams as quickly as possible! But how to achieve the goal of speed in telegrams is a very important question!

The process of a telegram from the sender to the telegraph office, from the telegraph office sending it, to its delivery to the recipient, has been roughly described by Mr. Jiran in the previous issue. In short, the conditions required for the speed of telegrams are the following four: (1) simple processing procedures, (2) sensitive telegraph machines, (3) intact telegraph lines, and (4) diligent staff. If the telegraph office can achieve all four of these, then the mission of speed in telegrams can be easily achieved. Conversely, if the telegraph office has a problem in any one of these aspects, telegrams will be difficult to expedite!

So, let's take a look at how the current telegraph office is doing with regard to the four items mentioned above. First, the Ministry of Communications has recently referenced the telegraph handling procedures of various foreign telegraph offices and commercially operated submarine cable companies, and used scientific methods to regulate the handling procedures. Under the principle of stability and reliability, it strives for simplicity of procedures so that handling can be expedited. Second, a year ago, the Ministry of Communications purchased a large number of new-style Creed telegraph machines, telegraph typewriters, and keyboard perforators from the United Kingdom, which will soon be installed in telegraph offices in Beijing, Shanghai, Tianjin, Wuhan, Beiping, Qingdao, Jinan, Yantai, Fuzhou, Xiamen, Guangdong, and other places. The advantage of this new-style Creed telegraph machine is that when the paper tape perforated in telegraph office A is sent to telegraph office B, telegraph office B also receives a perforated paper tape that is exactly the same. Telegraph office B then puts this paper tape on the machine and sends it to telegraph office C. If the old-style Western machine is used, then telegraph office B only receives a paper tape with symbols printed in ink. If it needs to be transferred to telegraph office C, only manual perforation can be used to punch the paper tape before sending it to telegraph office C. The new-style Creed machine can eliminate manual perforation, which can speed up the process by several times for long-distance telegrams that must be transferred through several telegraph offices. As for the telegraph typewriter, it is similar to an ordinary typewriter. This machine can be installed in telegraph offices with two direct telegraph lines. When telegraph office A types, telegraph office B immediately prints out the typed words, and its speed is the same as that of an ordinary typewriter. The keyboard perforator is also similar to a typewriter, but when the letter key is pressed, it can punch symbols on a kind of oiled paper tape, which is several times faster than manual perforation, which requires punching each dot and stroke. After these three types of machines are installed and used, the speed of telegrams will surely give the people of the country a new look! Third, the Ministry of Communications has been working hard to reorganize the telegraph lines in the past two years. Now, unless there is a strong wind or bandit disaster, there are few cases of interruption, so telegraph services are not delayed at all. Fourth, the Ministry of Communications has recently been sending personnel to inspect the diligence and laziness of telegraph office staff. Those who are found to be lazy or delaying telegrams are severely punished. Therefore, the spirit of doing things has been greatly invigorated recently. In particular, the people who receive telegrams have been repeatedly ordered to be humble in their attitude, so that the senders feel satisfied. At the same time, the telegraph office has also specially set up business inspectors to ask various merchants and telegram senders if there are any unsatisfactory points, so as to find out and improve them at any time. All four of the above-mentioned points have been put in a great deal of effort by the telegraph office in order to expedite telegrams. Now let me talk about how the senders and recipients of telegrams should help the telegraph office to achieve the mission of speed in telegrams!

If people who send Chinese telegrams translate the telegram into telegraph code themselves using the "New Compilation of Telegraph Codes," they will not only save translation fees, but also allow the telegram to be sent immediately when it is delivered to the telegraph office, saving the time of the telegraph office's translator to translate it into telegraph code. This is because the telegraph office's translators have at most two or three people per shift. If they receive more than a dozen Chinese telegrams at the same time, each person must translate three or four telegrams. In fact, the last telegram to be translated will inevitably be slightly delayed. This is the reason why the authorities have not abolished the translation fee to this day!

There are two things that recipients of telegrams can do to help the telegraph office to expedite telegram delivery: (1) When receiving a telegram, be sure to sign the receipt slip with the time of receipt. This will allow the person in charge of the telegraph office to know when the telegram was properly delivered. If there is an unjustified delay, the messenger can be punished as a warning to others. This will make the messengers not dare to delay the delivery of telegrams, and the telegram can be delivered to the recipient's hand quickly. (2) Recipients should preferably not detain the messenger, because each messenger usually carries two or three telegrams at a time when going out to deliver telegrams. If each recipient delays the messenger for several minutes, then the last telegram to be delivered will be delayed by ten or twenty minutes! At the same time, if a messenger is delayed outside for too long, he will be late returning to the office, so the remaining telegrams in the telegraph office will also be affected, because if he returns to the office one moment earlier, he can then deliver the remaining telegrams in turn! Although there are many messengers in the telegraph office, and there are several in each shift, all telegrams do not necessarily have to wait for a certain messenger to return to the office before they can be delivered. However, when the telegraph service is very busy, the faster the messenger returns to the office, the faster the delivery speed will be. This is an obvious fact. Speaking of the reasons why recipients detain messengers, there are roughly two reasons: First, the recipient is busy with other things and has no time to receive the telegram and sign. (Westerners often only sign, not stamp with a round seal.) Second, the recipient delays time because they are looking for a seal. Regarding these two points, (1) it is hoped that the recipient will sign for the telegram immediately when they receive it. (2) The personal seal should be kept on the body or in a certain place, so as to avoid wasting time looking for it temporarily. This will greatly benefit the telegraph office!

Recent Situation of Long-Distance Telephone in Europe and America 287

— Wang Qikun

I. Introduction

The connection of telephone networks and wireless telephone networks to form a world telephone network has been successfully realized. Countries are becoming increasingly concerned about the enrichment of their domestic telephone networks. Once technical problems are resolved through research, the trend is to focus on the establishment and completion of long-distance telephone circuit networks. Among these, Germany is particularly prominent, as the automation of its urban telephone system is nearing completion. It is now advancing toward the automation of long-distance telephones, which has become widespread. Many other small European countries have followed this example. In the United States, the American Telegraph and Telephone Company held a conference on long-distance telephone cable networks and accompanying plans in 1929, and the decisions made at the conference have been implemented sequentially. In the United States, telephone services in various states were originally handled by companies with different names under the same system. Now, this telephone network, especially long-distance telephone services, is directly managed by the American Telegraph and Telephone Company, so that the country can be unified and the design and maintenance can be gradually advanced according to plan.

II. Long-Distance Telephone in Germany

German telephone charges are based on distance, with a five-kilometer unit used as a charging zone. Calls within five kilometers (except for cities with more than 100,000 users, which can be extended to eight, ten, or fifteen kilometers depending on the number of users) are called ordinary urban calls, while those beyond this are called long-distance calls, which are further divided into short-distance calls (within 75 kilometers), medium-distance calls (within 300 kilometers), and long-distance calls (over 300 kilometers). Germany's investment in telephone equipment is shown in the table below, and its abundance of long-distance telephone cables and its sufficiency of long-distance telephone bureaus are highly noteworthy.

Land and property, Equipment inside the bureau, Underground cables, Overhead lines, Other, Total, Urban telephone, Million Marks, 194.1, 405.9, 557.5, 188.6, 62.7, 1409.8, Percentage, 13.8, 28.8, 39.6, 13.4, 4.4, 100.0, Long-distance telephone, Million Marks, 100.0, 60.9, 514.7, 110.5, 33.7, 819.8, Percentage, 16.7, 9.8, 50.3, 17.8, 5.4, 100.0

Long-distance telephones have the following three characteristics: (1) the call fee is calculated according to time and distance, (2) registration and waiting are required before the call, and (3) when a long-distance telephone is connected, if the user is making a local call, it is forcibly terminated. However, due to the gradual adoption of immediate dialing, the only difference between it and the urban telephone is the first item. The so-called immediate dialing means that, for example, when making a call from Nanjing to Zhenjiang, because there are many lines between Nanjing and Zhenjiang, the user can immediately connect from the Nanjing long-distance station to the Zhenjiang telephone bureau, or even directly transfer to the Zhenjiang bureau using the dialer on the telephone (such as Nanjing to Pukou) without going through the Nanjing long-distance station. Only after the Zhenjiang long-distance station makes an inquiry, it will connect to the user you want to reach. If the Zhenjiang telephone bureau is also automatic, the Nanjing user can completely directly call the Zhenjiang user.

Since the automation of urban telephones in Germany is nearing completion, its national long-distance telephone circuit network has also been completed, and the long-distance telephone bureaus have been merged and concentrated. Thus, a concentrated small long-distance bureau (E.F.) is used as a cell nucleus, and 55 suitable cities are selected nationwide as the first relay bureau (V.F.), and 15 places are the second relay bureau (D.F.). The domestic call area is also limited, and its lines can be connected to any place. The speech volume (Transmission Equivalent) of lines and bureau internal equipment is as follows:

Urban Telephone User to the bureau is 0.45N (that is, Noper), within the bureau is 0.15N, inter-bureau is 1N, totaling 2.2N.

Long-distance telephone (1) Urban part, user to urban bureau is 0.45N, urban bureau is 0.15N, urban bureau to long-distance bureau is 0.3N, long-distance bureau is 0.1N, totaling 1N, (2) Long-distance part, long-distance bureau and long-distance bureau is 1.3N, totaling 3.3N.

Immediate long-distance call, user to urban bureau is 0.45N, urban bureau is 0.15N, urban bureau to immediate bureau is 0.3N, immediate bureau is 0.25N, immediate bureau to immediate bureau is 1N, totaling 3.1N.

(A) Concentrated Small Long-Distance Bureau (E.F.)

Long-distance bureaus within a radius of about 35 kilometers are concentrated in the E.F. bureau at its center point. The exchange with the bureaus in this area is generally done in an immediate style. Calls between other bureaus in the area do not go through the operator and are fully automatic. Therefore, this inter-bureau connection line is not called a long-distance line. Immediate-style 50-week long-distance selection is used between adjacent E.F. bureaus.

(B) First Relay Bureau (V.F.)

Within the range where an intermediate repeater is not installed, this becomes the central bureau of the E.F. bureau, and an intermediate repeater is occasionally set up in special circumstances. Therefore, its coverage area is a radius of about 140 kilometers.

(C) Second Relay Bureau (D.F.)

This is equipped with the scale of a large long-distance bureau. All return lines from V.F. are concentrated here, and direct return lines are set up between each D.F. bureau. Due to geographical reasons, there are also international telephone bureaus set up here. Since it is connected to the cable network and is engaged in relaying overseas telephone calls, it is called the World Relay Bureau (V.F.), which is located in Berlin.

III. Long-Distance Telephone in the United Kingdom

Long-distance telephones in the United Kingdom are divided into 18 zones, which are further divided into 170 groups, each with a central bureau. This division is based on operational convenience and is not related to the charging area. Since 1930, Demand stations have been set up in the zone center bureaus to implement immediate dialing. There are direct lines between these bureaus. There are also direct lines from the group center bureaus to their affiliated zone center bureaus. The standard of voice volume such as inserting a middle repeater and the line is roughly as follows:

1. Between two users belonging to the same bureau, 2.2N.

2. Between users belonging to the same area, or different areas (within 340 kilometers), or two cities with direct lines, 2.7N

3. Between users in adjacent areas (more than 340 kilometers), places below 480 kilometers, or between users in two cities without direct lines and below 480 to 640 kilometers, 3.3N

4. Other long-distance long-distance telephone return lines, 3.9N

IV. Long-Distance Telephone in the United States

The United States, like Germany, also uses 2,500 bureaus as a central bureau, called Toll Center (T.C.), and its first relay bureau is called Primary outlet (P.O.), with 150 locations. These are also connected to eight Regional centers (R.C.) with direct lines, all of which use the immediate dialing of the C.L.R. method. Its voice volume is as follows:

T.C. P.O. 3. cdb T.C. T.C. 6. odb T.C. R. 3. 5db P.O. R. 3. 5db R.C. R.C. 4. 0db P.O. P.O. 4. 0db Direct line (for terminal bureau) 9.0db Terminal bureau loss 7.0db

The maximum loss when passing through two relay bureaus is 25 db (that is, decibeld b). The maximum voice volume between the United States and Canada is 31...

The structure of the long-distance telephone networks of the United Kingdom, the United States, and Germany is listed in the left for comparison:

Number of small long-distance bureaus, Number of first relay bureaus, Number of second relay bureaus, Number of world telephone bureaus, United Kingdom, Group Center 170, Zone center 18, 1, United States, Toll center 2500, Primary ooutlet 150, Regional acentr 8, Germany Bureau, E.F. 650, V.F. 55, D.F. 15, W.I.F

Bi-Weekly News 288

— Society Member

(Revised Three Types of Telegram Regulations) The Ministry of Communications believes that various telegram regulations have been promulgated for quite some time, and many of the articles are no longer suitable for use. Therefore, it has recently been revising various regulations one after another in order to be applicable. The three types of regulations that have now been revised and promulgated are the Zhenwu Telegram Regulations, the News Telegram Regulations, and the Postal Transfer Telegram Regulations. The content of the Zhenwu Telegram Regulations is roughly the same as the old Zhangwu Telegram Free Regulations, but the articles have been slightly reorganized. A new type of mid-way copy method has been added to the News Telegram Regulations. All news telegrams may be requested by the sender to be copied by the telegraph office that relays the telegram in the middle to the local news agencies (the telegraph office that does not relay the telegram in the middle cannot copy it. For example, Shanghai to Nanjing is a direct telegram, and Suzhou cannot copy it.) However, the words "Send to a certain news agency at a certain place" should be added in the recipient's name and address column. The charge for this copy telegram is one cent per Chinese character and two cents per English or Japanese character. The most important point of the revision of the Postal Transfer Telegram Regulations is the exemption of postage. The articles are simplified to make it easier for the public to understand. These new regulations can be obtained from various telegraph offices, radio stations, and this newspaper.

(Opening of the Sino-Japanese Wireless Circuit) The Sino-Japanese wireless circuit was officially opened on June 1. Shanghai has begun to receive and send foreign language, Chinese, and Japanese telegrams at the same time. The inland area is limited to receiving and sending foreign language telegrams. The communication radio stations are the Shanghai International Radio Station and the Tokyo Radio Station, both of which use high-speed automatic receiving and sending machines to work. Because the Tokyo Telegraph Bureau of Japan is the center of the Japanese telegraph lines, the telegrams are faster than those that must be relayed through Nagasaki by submarine cable. The charging methods for Chinese and Japanese telegrams are as follows:

(1) Name and address: The place name of the recipient and the recipient's name and address, regardless of how many characters, are all counted as one character. However, if a copy telegram adds one recipient's name and address, one character should be added.

(2) Telegram text: Chinese telegrams can be written with numbers connected together. For example, the two characters "Zhonghua" can be written as "00225478." Every seven numbers are counted as one character, which is more than twice or three times cheaper than the original charging method for foreign language telegrams (that is, four codes are counted as one character, and the recipient's name and address are charged by character). Japanese telegrams must be written in Japanese kana, and every seven kana are counted as one character. Detailed methods can be inquired at the Renji Road International Radio Station.

Q&A Column 289

— Reporter

(Mr. Li Yanzong asks) (1) Our place is 50 miles away from the city. Telegrams are delivered by letter carriers, and the public feels very difficult because they have to pay special labor fees. Can they all be delivered by postmen without taking additional fees?

(3) According to the new regulations, if the recipient's name and address do not exceed 15 characters, they are all charged according to five characters. How is it calculated if this number of characters is exceeded? Also, telegrams are not available in our county. Can we ask the post office to collect and forward telegrams on our behalf?

(Answer) (1) It is noted that telegrams marked for special delivery are sent immediately with one telegram and one messenger, so a special labor fee is charged. It is not convenient to have them all delivered by postmen to avoid delays. However, the collection of special labor fees has a certain set of regulations. Please read item (D) of the "Summary of New Regulations for Saving Telegram Fees" given by this newspaper to find out.

(2) Please read item (B) of the "Summary of New Regulations for Saving Telegram Fees" given by this newspaper to find out the method of calculating the fees for Chinese telegrams with the recipient's name and address exceeding 15 characters. If your county does not have a telegraph office, you can ask the post office to collect it on your behalf. This type of telegram is called a postal telegram transfer. At the post office, it is sent as an express letter, so it is also extremely fast. And from March 1, 1934, all fees are charged according to the prices set by the telegraph office, and no additional postage is charged.

(A gentleman from Wuxi asks) Can the following telegram be used as a clear telegram: (Jiangmi rose 122)? The telegraph office's receiver believed that the word "tube" in the telegram did not make sense and changed it to the two characters "per bag." Is this legal? Please show me.

(Answer) This telegram can be used as a clear code telegram. However, if the telegraph office's receiver has any doubts about the meaning of the telegram, the sender should explain it in detail to avoid misunderstandings. It is certainly illegal to change the telegram on behalf of the sender, and you can refuse the change.

Voices from the Telegraph Industry: Shanghai-Yantai-Gulin Submarine Cable 290

— Bing

Acting on behalf of returning to self-management

The Shanghai-Yantai-Gulin submarine cable has been managed by the Great Eastern and Great Northern Companies on behalf of the Chinese government starting from the 20th of this month, and has been returned to self-management *.

From then on, the convenience of telecommunications in the north of China will be further improved.

The areas through which the above-mentioned submarine cable passes are all within our country's territory and territorial waters. Independent communication is the only inviolable principle for independent countries in the world *.

However, in our country, there is the name of acting on behalf of the Chinese government. What does acting on behalf of the Chinese government mean? Is it not *

nominal but not real, and the power does not belong to us?

According to investigations, the Shanghai-Yantai-Gulin submarine cable was opportunistically laid by the Great Eastern and Great Northern Companies during the Boxer Rebellion because our country's Tianjin-Shanghai land line was sometimes blocked. After the matter was settled, the Qing court negotiated and established a treaty to repay the shallow capital in installments. The time *

was in the 26th year of Guangxu. According to the provisions of the treaty, it should have been recovered after the Western calendar year 1925 (that is, the 14th year of the Republic of China): Only because the situation was unstable in the past, it was indulged in and repeatedly delayed, which is inevitable *

is a pity.

The Shanghai-Yantai-Gulin submarine cable is extremely convenient for transmitting telegrams in northern China. Before it was recovered, it was parallel to our country's Tianjin-Shanghai direct land line and Shanghai-Yantai submarine cable, forming a confrontation: But in recent years, the Ministry of Communications has actively reorganized the Tianjin-Shanghai land line ( *

There is a section of submarine cable that is the Yangtze River) and the Shanghai-Yantai submarine cable is also well managed, and there are absolutely few drawbacks *

The profits were thick in the past, but they are thin today. Things are done by people, and it cannot be generalized.

Now that the Ministry of Communications has recovered the submarine cable for self-management, in the future, regarding the sending of telegrams to northern China, it can be done by land line. *

, and it is also possible by submarine cable. Originally, there was only one route, but now there are two routes for delivery, the efficiency is increased, and the speed is doubled. *

This is indeed the fact that can be shown after the submarine cable is recovered. As for the autonomy of communication rights, it is even more important, which is indeed worth *

to be pleased with.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Small Talk

El Salvador Recognizes the Puppet State 291

— Xing An

Given the Japanese's calculated, cunning schemes and international collusion, valuing profit over righteousness, we knew early on that those who would follow Japan in recognizing the puppet state would be numerous. Not long ago, there were rumors that Germany would recognize it, and legends that the United States would. Although neither country's recognition materialized, before we knew it, El Salvador, a small country in Central America, boldly and shamelessly violated international trust, infringed upon the League of Nations covenant, undermined the common front of various countries against Manchuria, and openly announced its recognition. According to reports: (The Republic of El Salvador, on the 19th of this month, notified Japan through its Consul General in Tokyo, and the representative of the Japanese puppet Manchuria, that the country officially recognized Manchuria from March 3rd of this year.)

According to the League of Nations resolution of March 11, 1932, non-recognition (of Manchuria) had long been on file. El Salvador, as a member of the League of Nations, though not voting at the time nor declaring abstention, was legally obligated to abide by that resolution. Now, disregarding everything, abandoning this mandatory obligation, and being the first to break the covenant and grant recognition, has a very serious impact on the fundamental issues of the League of Nations itself. According to the speculation of observers of the international situation in Washington: (El Salvador's recognition of (Manchuria) is nothing more than an attempt to make things difficult for the United States. Because El Salvador's interests in the Far East are insignificant, this action has no important significance other than making the United States' strategies towards neighboring countries slightly more thorny.) If this is true, we believe international behavior is far too frivolous. To vent personal resentment, any means are employed, even to the point of destroying the League of Nations covenant and leaving behind endless troubles, which is nothing less than being a thief of international morality. If the League of Nations does not severely punish and expel this irresponsible and despicable traitor in the future, then the League's remaining prestige will be completely lost.

However, in our opinion, although it is still difficult to understand the intention behind El Salvador's recognition of the puppet state, it may contain some element of embarrassment for the United States, as some Americans have suggested, but it can be asserted that it must have been secretly lured and manipulated by the Japanese. The Japanese have been visibly exhausted in their international attempts to have the puppet state of Manchukuo recognized. Up to now, although many major countries in the world have wanted to recognize it due to their interests, they have ultimately been hesitant to try it rashly due to some concerns. Therefore, in disappointment, the Japanese turned to winning over small countries like El Salvador, not hesitating to feign courteousness to induce them to recognize it. Because El Salvador is also a member of the League of Nations, its recognition, though not visibly enhancing the international status of the puppet Manchukuo, will certainly shake the League's anti-Manchuria front, which is enough to fulfill its long-cherished wish.

Regarding the issue of recognizing the puppet state, the future is not optimistic. According to the observation of the Paris Economic and Financial News Agency, (although the United States has used various roundabout means to isolate Japan, Japan is now taking the opportunity to strike back at the United States, and other Latin American countries may follow El Salvador's example.) We confirm this with the attitude previously taken by the United Kingdom, and we also know that those who will follow and recognize the puppet Manchukuo will surely follow one after another. The United Kingdom is the strongest supporter of the League of Nations, and it goes without saying that it should strictly abide by the League of Nations' resolution not to recognize the puppet state. However, when the United States and Japan advocated understanding in the past, London had a tendency to approve of the United States' recognition of the puppet Manchukuo, saying that (the United States' recognition of Manchuria is actually welcomed by the United Kingdom. The United Kingdom believes that the existence of Manchukuo is still far off, and Japan's hegemony in Manchuria is still difficult to shake for the time being. The United Kingdom is very close to the League of Nations, so the United Kingdom does not want the League of Nations to take a stand on Manchukuo, and it is the first to recognize it. However, the United Kingdom is willing for the United States to take steps to recognize Manchukuo, as a step for it to follow in the future.)

The puppet Manchukuo, created by the Japanese, has long been envied by the world. However, why have the countries decided not to recognize it in the past, and repeatedly wanted to recognize it later? This is exactly as the news agency said: (Whether Manchuria becomes a province of China or is protected by Japan, its future development is unlimited, which is known to everyone. Therefore, it is undoubtedly inevitable that countries will drool over it in the future. The reason why a small Central American country, which is now engaged in a diplomatic war with Washington, can overthrow the anti-Japanese resolution solemnly passed by the League of Nations is for this reason.) In other words, it is for the sake of profit. That is why we say that the future of the issue of recognizing the puppet state is not optimistic.

Regarding El Salvador's recognition of the puppet state, the plan for the future lies not in how the League of Nations will impose sanctions, or how the United States and Japan will re-emerge into conflict, but in how our country will be inspired and invigorated.

Season and Creativity 292

— Tian Hua

If spring is likened to a young girl, then summer should be a heavily made-up young woman. The bleak and solemn autumn easily makes us think of a late-blooming middle-aged woman, and the biting cold winter will awaken us to the loneliness of an old woman. Not only women, but most people's lives can be compared in this way. Although some people use a sound spirit as the standard, when talking about an elderly person, if he is progressive and combative, he can be an ("old youth"); a youth, if he lacks this passion and vitality, he is inevitably a ("remnant of the past"), who is mostly old. However, the passion of youth and the passion of old age are somewhat different after all, and youth after all has greater vitality. This is just like the seasons of spring and summer, which are likened to youth, and their contribution to mankind is greater after all, and cannot be compared with autumn and winter. The fallen leaves of autumn make us feel adrift, and the wind and snow of winter make us feel desolate. Only spring and summer, especially the late spring and early summer, give us the greatest vitality and creativity. During this period, we look at things with joyful eyes and work with an active and vigorous heart. At this time, our interest is particularly good, and our work efficiency is also particularly high! These are all bestowed upon us by the climate.

It is not difficult for us to find many examples. Many inventions and creations in the world have manifested their existence during these spring and summer seasons. May and June are particularly suitable for invention and creation. Columbus was convinced of the theory of a round earth and wanted to discover a route to India from the west, so he discovered the New World! But it was in May and June that he had this intention to sail. Galileo invented the telescope, and later used the telescope to observe the spots on the moon, saying that the moon has bumps and hollows like the earth, and is definitely not completely round! These inventions or discoveries were obtained through hard work in the months of April, May, and June. Goethe's Faust was written in March and April. Many of Dante's poems were also mostly written in the spring and summer seasons. Someone, based on the months and years of many masterpieces in the world, said that May is the most suitable month for creation in the four seasons of the year, followed by April, June, March (March and June are the same), September, July, and August. The months that are not suitable for creation are November, January, October, December, and February! Among them, February is the worst and cannot be created. From the above facts, we know that we are now in the most active month of May, in this ("eventful") month of May. In fact, the reason why May is ("eventful") is precisely to give us a powerful proof that May is the most active and vibrant month for people. Workers all over the world show their vitality on the very first day of May. May 3rd, May 4th, May 9th, and May 30th each represent the most active link of people in this month. I dare say that in the future, major changes in the world, such as major revolutions, major wars, and major... will have more opportunities to occur in May and its neighboring months. The influence of the season on people is undeniable.

In fact, this is almost self-evident. In the spring and summer seasons, birds sing particularly well, and their feathers are also more beautiful. During this period, animals are particularly majestic and spectacular. At this time, human faces also show particularly vivid and lively smiles, and their hearts are filled with vitality and spring feelings! Everything shows the greatness of the season's bestowal.

We must not fail such a good season, let us all unleash our potential vitality and creativity!
